												<div class="content-container-inner">
				<a name="content"></a>
																<div class="search-filters clearfix"><div class="ajax_filter_wrapper search_filters">
											<form class="ajax_filter_form">
							<div class="ajax_filters">
																	<div class="ajax_keyword_filter">
											<input type="text" id="jobfilters_keywords_" size="30" minlength="0" maxlength="255" no_submit="" placeholder="Find jobs by job title, company, location and more" name="jobfilters[keywords]" value="" class="input-text ui-autocomplete-input" autocomplete="off" /><span role="status" aria-live="polite" class="ui-helper-hidden-accessible"></span>
																<a href="javascript:;" class="search_help_icon search_help_button icn-help">Help</a>
						<div class="help_box">
    <div class="help_box_header">
        <a href="javascript:;" class="help_box_close help_box_close_button icon_16 icon_close ti-close">Close</a>
        <p>Advanced Usage</p>
    </div>

    <div class="help_box_body">
        <div>
            <p class="help_box_title">The search will be performed on the following sections in order of relevancy:</p>
            <label class="help_box_label order">Job Id &gt; employer &gt; Job Title &gt; Location &gt; Description</label>
        </div>

        <div>
            <p class="help_box_title">The search capability supports the following operators:</p>
            <p>
                <span class="help_box_example">+</span>
                <label class="help_box_label">A leading plus sign indicates that this word must be present (AND).</label>
            </p>
            <p>
                <span class="help_box_example">-</span>
                <label class="help_box_label">A leading minus sign indicates that this word must not be present (NOT).</label>
            </p>
            <p>
                <span class="help_box_example">(no operator)</span>
                <label class="help_box_label">If no operator is used items that match more words will be rated higher (OR).</label>
            </p>
            <p> 
                <span class="help_box_example">( )</span>
                <label class="help_box_label">Parentheses are used to group words into subexpressions and can be nested. Use explicit &amp;&amp; for AND, || for OR, ! for NOT. </label>
            </p>
            <p>
                <span class="help_box_example">" "</span>
                <label class="help_box_label">A phrase that is enclosed within double quote ( " " ) characters matches only items that contain the phrase.</label>
            </p>
            <p>
                <span class="help_box_example">?</span>
                <label class="help_box_label">Use in place of any one character (can not be used in the beginning of the word).</label>
            </p>
            <p>
                <span class="help_box_example">*</span>
                <label class="help_box_label">Use in place of zero, one or multiple characters (can not be used in the beginning of the word).</label>
            </p>
        </div>
        
        <div>
            <p class="help_box_title">Examples:</p>
            <p>
                <span class="help_box_example">apple banana</span>
                <label class="help_box_label">Find items that contain at least one of the two words.</label>
            </p>
            <p>
                <span class="help_box_example">+apple +juice</span>
                <label class="help_box_label">Find items that contain both words.</label>
            </p>
            <p>
                <span class="help_box_example">+apple macintosh</span>
                <label class="help_box_label">Find items that contain the word "apple", but rank items higher if they also contain "macintosh".</label>
            </p>
             <p>
                <span class="help_box_example">+apple ‑macintosh</span>
                <label class="help_box_label">Find items that contain the word "apple" but not "macintosh".</label>
            </p>
            <p>
                <span class="help_box_example">"some words"</span>
                <label class="help_box_label">Find items that contain the exact phrase "some words" (for example, rows that contain "some words of wisdom" but not "some noise words").</label>
            </p>
            <p>
                <span class="help_box_example">apple*</span>
                <label class="help_box_label">Find items that contain words such as "apple", "apples", "applesauce", or "applet".</label>
            </p>
            <p>
                <span class="help_box_example">te?t</span>
                <label class="help_box_label">Matches words like "text" or "test" but not "tempt".</label>
            </p>
       </div>
    </div>

</div>										<input type="submit" value="search" class="ajax_filter_submit input-submit" />

function printPreview(warn) {
  var confirmation = true;
  if (warn == true) {
    confirmation = confirm('Only saved data will be printed. Click OK to continue or Cancel to go back and save first.');
  }
  if (confirmation) {
    window.open('/students/index.php?_do_print=1&amp;print_v=1494123538','printer_friendly','location=0,menubar=1,toolbar=1,resizable=1,scrollbars=1');
  } else {
    return false;
  }
}

var shouldprint = false;

function printQuick() {
  
    frame = frames['__hiddenframe'+nextFrame()];
    frame.location.href = '/students/index.php?_do_print=1&amp;_do_print_quick=1&amp;version=1494123538';
    shouldprint = true;
}
function printMeOnce(frame) {
  if (shouldprint) {
    frame.focus();
	if (typeof(frame.window.print) == 'function') {
	  frame.window.print();
        }
        else {
          print();
        }
  }
}
